Using your finger, stir gently to hydrate. Let the mixture sit for a couple of minutes, until foam begins to form.\n2.  **Add Oil and Initial Flour:** Add the olive oil to the mixture. Then add two tablespoons of flour to the mixing bowl, and mix on low speed.\n3. **Incorporate honey or sugar:** Add the honey or sugar and continue mixing.\n4. **Add the flour:** Add about four more tablespoons of flour and continue to mix on low speed, gradually adding flour until well combined. Then add the salt.\n5. **Mix the Dough:** Mix on low speed until the dough begins to come together. Increase the speed to medium and continue to mix the dough until it begins to form a cohesive ball.\n6. **Bulk Fermentation:** Lightly grease a large bowl, either with oil or cooking spray. Then transfer the dough ball to the bowl. Cover the bowl with an airtight lid or plastic wrap and let it rise in the refrigerator for at least 12 hours, ideally up to 48 hours.\n7. **Divide and Shape the Dough:** Remove the bulk dough from the refrigerator. Lightly flour a work surface and turn the dough out. Cut the dough into 9.5-ounce balls, using a digital scale for precision.\n8. **Shape the Dough:** Form the dough balls, using your hands to smooth the top of the dough and create a smooth round ball. Place the dough balls in individual, lightly oiled containers.\n9. **Second Fermentation:** Let the dough balls rest in the refrigerator for at least 2 days. This fermentation period is important for the quality of your pizza dough. \n10. **Prepare the Toppings:** While the dough is fermenting, prepare your toppings, such as pepperoni, bacon, and cheese. Cut the pepperoni into slices, grate the mozzarella cheese.\n11. **Shape the Pizza:** When ready to bake, remove the dough ball from the refrigerator. On a floured surface, use your hands to gently press the dough into a disc, leaving a raised border for the crust. Then throw the disc into the air to create a more circular shape.\n12. **Top the Pizza:** Use a pizza peel, place the dough disc on top. Add your sauce, mozzarella cheese, sliced pepperoni, and bacon pieces to the pizza. \n13. **Bake the Pizza:** Bake the pizza in a hot pizza oven. Remove when the crust is golden brown and the cheese is melted.\n14. **Serve:** Allow the pizza to rest on a pizza stone for a few minutes.
